Pkgs on Nix

Curated information about every package on Nix!

nixpkgs / coq_8_12 - Coq is a formal proof management system. It provides a formal language to write mathematical definitions, executable algorithms and theorems together with an environment for semi-interactive development of machine-checked proofs.

Homepage - http://coq.inria.fr

License - LGPL-2.1

Maintainers - Russell O'Connor - Austin Seipp - Vincent Laporte - Th√©o Zimmermann
